The '''sixth season''' of Philippine amateur singing competition '''''[[Tawag ng Tanghalan]]''''', titled '''''Tawag ng Tanghalan: Ika-anim na Taon''''', was an amateur singing competition aired as a  segment of the noontime variety television show ''[[It's Showtime (Philippine TV program)|It's Showtime]]''.<ref>{{Cite web|title=Magpasikat 2021: 'Showtime' to celebrate 12th anniversary on November 27|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/11/08/21/happy-12th-showtime-magpasikat-2021-finally-set|date=November 8, 2021|access-date=November 9, 2021|website=[[ABS-CBN News and Current Affairs|ABS-CBN News]]|language=en}}</ref> The segment premiered from November 22, 2021 to May 6, 2023.

From January 6 to 15, 2022, daily live production of It's Showtime was halted due to the surge of [[COVID-19 pandemic in the Philippines|COVID-19 cases]] caused by the [[SARS-CoV-2 Omicron variant|Omicron variant]]. The season resumed on January 17, 2022.<ref>{{Cite web|title='It's Showtime' resumes live broadcast after 10-day break due to COVID-19|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/01/17/22/its-showtime-resumes-live-broadcast-after-10-day-break|date=January 17, 2022|access-date=January 18, 2022|website=ABS-CBN News|language=en}}</ref>

From July 15, 2022 to April 29, 2023, the airtime of this segment was temporarily shortened due to 45 minutes of It's Showtime's airtime being given to ''[[Tropang LOL]]''.<ref>{{Cite web|title='It's Showtime' returns to 12 noon timeslot|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/05/01/23/its-showtime-returns-to-12-noon-timeslot
|date=May 1, 2023|access-date=May 1, 2023|website=news.abs-cbn.com}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|title=Tropang LOL, magpapaalam na sa ere sa April 29 — sources|url=https://www.pep.ph/pepalerts/pep-troika/172315/tropang-lol-to-bid-goodbye-on-tv5-a2z-a4118-20230324|website=Philippine Entertainment Portal|date=March 24, 2023|access-date=March 26, 2023|language=tl}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|title=Confirmed na! Pagbabu ng Tropang LOL sa ere, may petsa na, ikinalungkot nina Alex G, Billy Crawford atbp|url=https://balita.net.ph/2023/03/25/confirmed-na-pagbabu-ng-tropang-lol-sa-ere-may-petsa-na-ikinalungkot-nina-alex-g-billy-crawford-atbp|website=Balita|date=March 25, 2023|access-date=March 26, 2023|language=tl}}</ref>

Additionally, this season of Tawag ng Tanghalan is considered as the longest of all its seasons and probably the longest competition in the world as it lasted for a year and six months.

== Changes ==
The mechanics for the daily rounds for this season were modified. In the first round, dubbed as "Battle of Versions," daily contenders perform the same song with their renditions. The winners of the first round advance to the second round, dubbed as the "Face-off," where contestants perform a song of their choice to snatch the golden microphone from the defending champion. The champion who defends their title five times advances to the quarterfinals, whereas reaching the eighth time automatically grants them a place in the semifinals.<ref>{{Cite web|title=Tawag ng Tanghalan hopefuls now have to sing different versions of the same song in new format|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/11/22/21/watch-new-format-as-tawag-ng-tanghalan-launches-6th-year|first1=Miguel|last1=Dumaual|date=November 22, 2021|access-date=November 22, 2021|website=[[ABS-CBN News and Current Affairs|ABS-CBN News]]|language=en}}</ref>

== Hosts and judges ==
[[Vhong Navarro]], [[Vice Ganda]], [[Amy Perez]], and [[Kim Chiu]] reprised their roles as hosts, with [[Karylle]], [[Ion Perez]], [[Ogie Alcasid]], and Jackie Gonzaga as the rotating fifth co-host. [[Anne Curtis]] and [[Jhong Hilario]] both returned to their hosting duties in May and June after their respective hiatuses.

[[Ryan Bang]] reprised his role as gong master with substitutes [[Jameson Blake]] and [[Maymay Entrata]], and [[Itchyworms|Jugs Jugueta]], and [[Teddy Corpuz]] appeared in past roles occasionally.

Jugueta, Corpuz and Perez returned as backstage hosts.

[[Louie Ocampo]], [[Ogie Alcasid]], [[Zsa Zsa Padilla]], [[Erik Santos]], [[Klarisse de Guzman]], [[Nyoy Volante]], [[Jed Madela]], [[Karylle]], [[Yeng Constantino]], [[Kyla (Filipino singer)|Kyla]], [[Angeline Quinto]], and [[Jolina Magdangal]] returned as judges for the sixth season.

[[Marco Sison]], [[Darren Espanto]], and [[Jona Viray]] joined the judging panel on November 1, 2022,<ref>{{Cite web|title=Marco Sison joins 'It's Showtime' as 'Tawag ng Tanghalan' judge|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/11/02/22/marco-sison-now-a-tawag-ng-tanghalan-judge|date=November 2, 2022|access-date=May 12, 2023|website=ABS-CBN News|language=en}}</ref> February 21, 2023<ref>{{Cite web|title=Darren Espanto joins 'Showtime' as new 'Tawag ng Tanghalan' judge|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/02/21/23/darren-joins-showtime-as-tawag-ng-tanghalan-judge|date=February 21, 2023|access-date=May 12, 2023|website=ABS-CBN News|language=en}}</ref> and April 17, 2023<ref>{{Cite web|title=Jona is new 'Tawag ng Tanghalan' judge|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/04/17/23/jona-is-new-tawag-ng-tanghalan-judge|date=April 17, 2023|access-date=May 12, 2023|website=ABS-CBN News|language=en}}</ref> respectively.

Starting from May 1, 2023, the amount of judges returned to 5 judges for the first time since the [[COVID-19 pandemic in the Philippines]] implemented restrictions that caused the amount of judges to be reduced to 3 judges.

[[Randy Santiago]], [[Rey Valera]], and [[K Brosas]] did not return due to their commitments to [[Sing Galing (2021 TV program)|Sing Galing]]. Past judges [[Karla Estrada]] and [[Mitoy Yonting]] also did not return. However, [[Gary Valenciano]], reprised his role for the grand finale.

== Prizes ==
The defending champion receives {{Philippine peso|10,000}} while the losing contenders receive {{Philippine peso|5,000}}.

Ryan Ayangco (Luzon), who became a defending champion on January 3, 2022, withdrew from the competition the next day due to health 
reasons. Patricia Ivy Peñano (Luzon), who became a defending champion on January 4, 2022, also withdrew from the competition on the next week due to health reasons. They both returned on March 12, 2022.

== Quarter-finals ==
This format is similar to the [[Tawag ng Tanghalan (season 5)#Quarter Finals|Quarter Finals of season 5]]. The quarter finalists are scored of the following criteria: Voice quality (50%) and Overall performance (50%).

=== Quarter I ===
The 8 Quarter Finalists (now 7), will compete in a head to head battle. They had the power to choose the song of their competitor from a random selection of songs of their opponents. The Top 2 Quarter Finalists with the highest scores at the end of the week will move on to the semifinals and will receive {{Philippine peso|25,000}}. A consolation prize of {{Philippine peso|10,000}} is given to quarter finalists who failed to advance to the next round. The First Quarter Finals week aired on April 4—9, 2022.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/entertainment/04/05/22/close-fight-kicks-off-tawag-ng-tanghalan-quarterfinals|title=WATCH: Close fight kicks off tension-filled 'Tawag ng Tanghalan' quarterfinals|website=[[ABS-CBN News and Current Affairs|ABS-CBN News]]|date=April 5, 2022|access-date=August 16, 2022}}</ref>

Eufritz Santos (Metro Manila) from [[Tawag ng Tanghalan (season 5)|fifth season]], who withdrew at that time due to health reasons, will compete in  Quarter I Quarter Finals Week.

Querubin Llavore (Mindanao) did not perform in the competition due to health reasons, but she will return in the next quarter finals.

* {{Color box|#FAFAD2|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist advanced to the Semifinals
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was eliminated

=== Quarter II ===
The 8 Quarter Finalists, will compete in a head to head battle. It follows the same mechanics of the First Quarter Finals Week. They had the power to choose the song of their competitors from a random selection of songs of their opponents. The Top 2 Quarter Finalists with the highest scores at the end of the week will move to the Semifinals and will receive {{Philippine peso|25,000}}. A consolation prize of {{Philippine peso|10,000}} will be given to quarter finalists who failed to advance to the next round. The Second Quarter Finals Week was aired on October 10–15, 2022.

Querubin Llavore (Mindanao), did not perform in the competition, but she will compete in Quarter II ''Resbakbakan'' Week.

==== Daily Rounds ====
'''Results Details'''{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}
{{plainlist|* {{Color box|#FDFC8F|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist advanced to the next round
* {{Color box|#B0E0E6|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist lost in the Head to Head Battle but was given a second chance by the judges
* {{Color box|#FAFAD2|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist advanced to the Semifinals
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was eliminated
* {{Color box|#a0a0a0|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist withdrew from the competition}}
{{col-end}}

=== Quarter III ===
The 7 Quarter Finalists, will compete in a single round elimination for five days. The Quarter Finalist who got the lowest score for the specific day will be eliminated from the competition. The Top 2 Quarter Finalists with the highest scores at the end of the week will move to the Semifinals and will receive {{Philippine peso|25,000}}. A consolation prize of {{Philippine peso|10,000}} will be given to quarter finalists who failed to advance to the next round. The Third Quarter Finals Week was aired on April 17–22, 2023.

==== Daily Rounds ====
'''Results Details'''{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}

* {{Color box|#B0E0E6|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist lost in the Head to Head Battle but was given a second chance by the judges
* {{Color box|#FAFAD2|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist advanced to the Semifinals
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist was eliminated
* {{Color box|#a0a0a0|border=silver}} Quarter Finalist withdrew from the competition}}
{{col-end}}

=== Quarter I ===
The 12 ''Resbakers'', (six daily winners, three 2-time defending champions and three 4-time defending champions), divided into two groups of six will perform their redemption songs. The Top 3 Resbakers on Monday and Tuesday will advance on Wednesday. The Final 6 Resbakers will compete for 2 rounds and the Top 3 Resbakers will have the chance to advance to get the Top 2 spots for the ''Ultimate Resbak'' Week.

'''Results Details'''{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}
{{plainlist|* {{Color box|#f7cb52|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the Ultimate Resbak
* {{Color box|#FDFD96|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the next round
* {{Color box|pink|border=silver}}  Resbaker belonged to the Top 3, but was switched out and eliminated
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}}  Resbaker was eliminated
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Resbaker was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|#a0a0a0|border=silver}} Resbaker withdrew from the competition}}
{{col-end}}

=== Quarter II ===
The 12 ''Resbakers'', (three daily winners, two 1-time defending champions, two 2- time defending champions, two 3-time defending champions, two 4-time defending champions and one Quarterfinalist), will perform their redemption songs in a head to head battle. The remaining 6 Resbakers will compete in a head to head battle again. The Top 4 Resbakers will get the chance to advance to get the Top 2 spots for the ''Ultimate Resbak'' Round.

'''Results Details'''{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}
{{plainlist|* {{Color box|#f7cb52|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the Ultimate Resbak
* {{Color box|#FDFD96|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the next round
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}}  Resbaker was eliminated
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Resbaker was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|#a0a0a0|border=silver}} Resbaker withdrew from the competition}}
{{col-end}}

=== Quarter III ===
The 12 ''Resbakers'', (five daily winners, three 1-time defending champions,  three 2-time defending champions and one 3-time defending champion), divided into four groups of three  will perform their redemption songs. The Resbakers with the highest score from Monday to Thursday will advance to the final round on Friday. The Top 4 Resbakers will have a chance to advance to get the Top 2 spots for the ''Ultimate Resbak'' Round on Saturday together with the ''Ultimate Resbakers'' from Quarter I and Quarter II.

'''Results Details'''{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}
{{plainlist|* {{Color box|#f7cb52|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the Ultimate Resbak
* {{Color box|#FDFD96|border=silver}} Resbaker advanced to the next round
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}}  Resbaker was eliminated
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} Resbaker was 'gonged' and eliminated
* {{Color box|#a0a0a0|border=silver}} Resbaker withdrew from the competition}}
{{col-end}}

== Ultimate ''Resbak'' ==
The 7 Ultimate ''Resbakers'' will perform their redemption songs for 2 rounds. The Top 2 Resbakers will have the chance to advance to the second round. The Ultimate ''Resbaker'' with the highest score will advance to the Semifinals and will receive {{Philippine peso|25,000}}. A consolation prize of {{Philippine peso|10,000}} will be given to Ultimate ''Resbakers'' who failed to advance to the next round.

{{col-begin}}
{{col-4}}
{{plainlist|* {{Color box|#FAFAD2|border=silver}} ''Ultimate Resbaker'' advanced to the Semifinals
* {{Color box|#FDFD96|border=silver}} ''Ultimate Resbaker'' advanced to the next round 
* {{Color box|salmon|border=silver}} ''Ultimate Resbaker'' was eliminated
* {{Color box|#CD5C5C|border=silver}} ''Ultimate Resbaker'' was 'gonged' and eliminated}}
{{col-end}}

=== Semifinal Details ===
The Semifinal round airs on May 1 to 5, 2023. For the first four days, the twelve semifinalists are divided into four groups. Each day, a group of three contenders performs a three-way battle performance, followed by a solo performance. The contender garnering the highest average score of the day advances directly to the Grand Finals. Additionally, the judges can vote on a conteder that will be saved from elimination. The four ''hurado's'' save shall advance on the Friday round.

For the first time since the [[Tawag ng Tanghalan (season 3)|third season]], there is a homecoming and [[featurette]] for the semifinalists due to the eased COVID-19 restrictions after nearly two and a half years under pandemic-induced restrictions. Additionally, the judging panel reverted back to five judges for the first time since the pandemic episodes.

{{col-2}}

{{col-end}}
